[Code Examples](#code-examples)\n7. [Webhooks](#webhooks)\n8. [SDKs](#sdks)\n\n---\n\n## Introduction\n\n### Base URL\n```\nhttps://api.prooflink.ai/v1\n```\n\n### API Version\nCurrent version: `v1`\n\n### Content Type\nAll requests and responses use JSON:\n```\nContent-Type: application/json\n```\n\n### HTTPS Required\nAll API requests must be made over HTTPS. HTTP requests will be rejected.\n\n---\n\n## Authentication\n\n### API Keys\n\nProofLink uses API keys for authentication. Include your API key in the `Authorization` header:\n\n```bash\nAuthorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY\n```\n\n### Getting Your API Key\n\n1. Log in to your ProofLink dashboard\n2. Navigate to Settings ‚Üí API Keys\n3. Click "Create New API Key"\n4. Copy and securely store your key\n\n### Security Best Practices\n\n- Never commit API keys to version control\n- Store keys in environment variables\n- Rotate keys regularly\n- Use different keys for different environments\n- Revoke compromised keys immediately\n\n---\n\n## Endpoints\n\n### Authentication\n\n#### Register User\n```http\nPOST /auth/register\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "user@example.com",\n  "password": "SecurePassword123!",\n  "name": "John Doe"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "user_123",\n  "email": "user@example.com",\n  "name": "John Doe",\n  "access_token": "eyJhbGc...",\n  "refresh_token": "eyJhbGc...",\n  "token_type": "bearer"\n}\n```\n\n#### Login\n```http\nPOST /auth/login\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "user@example.com",\n  "password": "SecurePassword123!"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "access_token": "eyJhbGc...",\n  "refresh_token": "eyJhbGc...",\n  "token_type": "bearer",\n  "expires_in": 3600\n}\n```\n\n#### Refresh Token\n```http\nPOST /auth/refresh\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "refresh_token": "eyJhbGc..."\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "access_token": "eyJhbGc...",\n  "token_type": "bearer",\n  "expires_in": 3600\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Proofs\n\n#### Create Proof\n```http\nPOST /proofs\n```\n\n**Headers:**\n```\nAuthorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY\nContent-Type: multipart/form-data\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```\nfile: [binary file data]\nfilename: "document.pdf" (optional)\ndescription: "Contract for Project X" (optional)\ntags: ["contract", "2024"] (optional)\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "proof_abc123",\n  "filename": "document.pdf",\n  "file_hash": "a3d5e7f9...",\n  "proof_link": "https://prooflink.ai/verify/abc123",\n  "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",\n  "file_size": 1048576,\n  "mime_type": "application/pdf"\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Proof\n```http\nGET /proofs/{proof_id}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "proof_abc123",\n  "filename": "document.pdf",\n  "file_hash": "a3d5e7f9...",\n  "proof_link": "https://prooflink.ai/verify/abc123",\n  "verification_count": 42,\n  "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",\n  "expires_at": null,\n  "is_active": true,\n  "file_size": 1048576,\n  "mime_type": "application/pdf",\n  "metadata": {\n    "description": "Contract for Project X",\n    "tags": ["contract", "2024"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### List Proofs\n```http\nGET /proofs\n```\n\n**Query Parameters:**\n- `page`: Page number (default: 1)\n- `limit`: Results per page (default: 20, max: 100)\n- `status`: Filter by status (`active`, `expired`)\n- `search`: Search by filename\n- `sort`: Sort by (`created_at`, `filename`, `verifications`)\n- `order`: Sort order (`asc`, `desc`)\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "data": [\n    {\n      "id": "proof_abc123",\n      "filename": "document.pdf",\n      "file_hash": "a3d5e7f9...",\n      "proof_link": "https://prooflink.ai/verify/abc123",\n      "verification_count": 42,\n      "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",\n      "is_active": true\n    }\n  ],\n  "pagination": {\n    "page": 1,\n    "limit": 20,\n    "total": 150,\n    "pages": 8\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Delete Proof\n```http\nDELETE /proofs/{proof_id}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "message": "Proof deleted successfully"\n}\n```\n\n#### Batch Create Proofs\n```http\nPOST /proofs/batch\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "files": [\n    {\n      "filename": "doc1.pdf",\n      "file_data": "base64_encoded_data"\n    },\n    {\n      "filename": "doc2.pdf",\n      "file_data": "base64_encoded_data"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "proofs": [\n    {\n      "id": "proof_abc123",\n      "filename": "doc1.pdf",\n      "proof_link": "https://prooflink.ai/verify/abc123"\n    },\n    {\n      "id": "proof_def456",\n      "filename": "doc2.pdf",\n      "proof_link": "https://prooflink.ai/verify/def456"\n    }\n  ],\n  "total": 2,\n  "successful": 2,\n  "failed": 0\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Verification\n\n#### Verify File\n```http\nPOST /verify/{proof_link}\n```\n\n**Headers:**\n```\nContent-Type: multipart/form-data\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```\nfile: [binary file data]\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "is_valid": true,\n  "proof_id": "proof_abc123",\n  "filename": "document.pdf",\n  "file_hash": "a3d5e7f9...",\n  "verified_at": "2024-01-15T11:00:00Z",\n  "message": "File verification successful"\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Verification History\n```http\nGET /proofs/{proof_id}/verifications\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "data": [\n    {\n      "id": "ver_xyz789",\n      "verified_at": "2024-01-15T11:00:00Z",\n      "is_valid": true,\n      "ip_address": "192.168.1.1",\n      "user_agent": "Mozilla/5.0..."\n    }\n  ],\n  "total": 42\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### User Management\n\n#### Get Current User\n```http\nGET /users/me\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "user_123",\n  "email": "user@example.com",\n  "name": "John Doe",\n  "created_at": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z",\n  "subscription": {\n    "plan": "pro",\n    "status": "active",\n    "expires_at": "2024-02-01T00:00:00Z"\n  },\n  "stats": {\n    "total_proofs": 150,\n    "total_verifications": 1234,\n    "api_calls_today": 45\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Update User\n```http\nPUT /users/me\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "name": "John Smith",\n  "timezone": "America/New_York",\n  "notifications_enabled": true\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "user_123",\n  "email": "user@example.com",\n  "name": "John Smith",\n  "timezone": "America/New_York",\n  "notifications_enabled": true\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### API Keys\n\n#### List API Keys\n```http\nGET /users/api-keys\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "data": [\n    {\n      "id": "key_abc123",\n      "name": "Production ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Create API Key\n```http\nPOST /users/api-keys\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "name": "Development Server"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "id": "key_def456",\n /analytics/overview\n```\n\n**Query Parameters:**\n- `start_date`: Start date (ISO 8601)\n- `end_date`: End date (ISO 8601)\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "total_proofs": 150,\n ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Error Response Format\n\n```json\n{\n  "error": {\n    "code": "invalid_request",\n    "message": "The request is missing required parameters",\n    "details": {\n      "missing_fields": ["email", "password"]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### HTTP Status Codes\n\n| Code | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| 200 | Success |\n| 201 | Created |\n| 400 | Bad Request |\n| 401 | Unauthorized |\n| 403 | Forbidden |\n| 404 | Not Found |\n| 429 | Too Many Requests |\n| 500 | Internal Server Error |\n\n### Error Codes\n\n| Code | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| `invalid_request` | Request is malformed or missing required fields |\n| `authentication_failed` | Invalid credentials or API key |\n| `unauthorized` | Valid credentials but insufficient permissions |\n| `not_found` | Resource does not exist |\n| `rate_limit_exceeded` | Too many requests |\n| `file_too_large` | File exceeds size limit |\n| `invalid_file_type` | File type not supported |\n| `verification_failed` | File verification failed |\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limits\n\n### Limits by Plan\n\n| Plan | Requests/Hour | Requests/Day |\n|------|---------------|--------------|\n| Free | 100 | 1,000 |\n| Pro | 1,000 | 10,000 |\n| Enterprise | Custom | Custom |\n\n### Rate Limit Headers\n\n```\nX-RateLimit-Limit: 1000\nX-RateLimit-Remaining: 999\nX-RateLimit-Reset: 1642262400\n```\n\n### Handling Rate Limits\n\nWhen rate limited, you\'ll receive a 429 status code:\n\n```json\n{\n  "error": {\n    "code": "rate_limit_exceeded",\n    "message": "Rate limit exceeded. Try again in 3600 seconds.",\n    "retry_after": 3600\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Code Examples\n\n### Python\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\nAPI_KEY = "your_api_key_here"\nBASE_URL = "https://api.prooflink.ai/v1"\n\nheaders = {\n    "Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}",\n    "Content-Type": "application/json"\n}\n\n# Create a proof\nwith open("document.pdf", "rb") as file:\n    files = {"file": file}\n    response = requests.post(\n        f"{BASE_URL}/proofs",\n        headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}"},\n        files=files\n    )\n    proof = response.json()\n    print(f"Proof created: {proof[\'proof_link\']}")\n\n# Verify a file\nwith open("document.pdf", "rb") as file:\n    files = {"file": file}\n    response = requests.post(\n        f"{BASE_URL}/verify/abc123",\n        files=files\n    )\n    result = response.json()\n    print(f"Valid: {result[\'is_valid\']}")\n```\n\n### JavaScript (Node.js)\n\n```javascript\nconst axios = require(\'axios\');\nconst FormData = require(\'form-data\');\nconst fs = require(\'fs\');\n\nconst API_KEY = \'your_api_key_here\';\nconst BASE_URL = \'https://api.prooflink.ai/v1\';\n\n// Create a proof\nasync function createProof(filePath) {\n  const form = new FormData();\n  form.append(\'file\', fs.createReadStream(filePath));\n\n  const response = await axios.post(`${BASE_URL}/proofs`, form, {\n    headers: {\n      \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${API_KEY}`,\n      ...form.getHeaders()\n    }\n  });\n\n  console.log(\'Proof created:\', response.data.proof_link);\n  return response.data;\n}\n\n// Verify a file\nasync function verifyFile(proofLink, filePath) {\n  const form = new FormData();\n  form.append(\'file\', fs.createReadStream(filePath));\n\n  const response = await axios.post(\n    `${BASE_URL}/verify/${proofLink}`,\n    form,\n    { headers: form.getHeaders() }\n  );\n\n  console.log(\'Valid:\', response.data.is_valid);\n  return response.data;\n}\n```\n\n### cURL\n\n```bash\n# Create a proof\ncurl -X POST https://api.prooflink.ai/v1/proofs \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY" \\\n  -F "file=@document.pdf"\n\n# Verify Navigate to Settings ‚Üí Webhooks\n2. Click "Add Webhook"\n3. Enter your endpoint URL\n4. Select events to subscribe to\n5. Save webhook\n\n### Webhook Events\n\n- `proof.created`: New proof created\n- `proof.deleted`: Proof deleted\n- `verification.completed`: File verified\n- `verification.failed`: Verification failed\n\n### Webhook Payload\n\n```json\n{\n  "event": "verification.completed",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T12:00:00Z",\n  "data": {\n    "proof_id": "proof_abc123",\n    "verification_id": "ver_xyz789",\n    "is_valid": true,\n    "verified_at": "2024-01-15T12:00:00Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Webhook Security\n\nVerify webhook signatures using the `X-ProofLink-Signature` header:\n\n```python\nimport hmac\nimport hashlib\n\ndef verify_webhook(payload, signature, secret):\n    expected = hmac.new(\n        secret.encode(),\n        payload.encode(),\n        hashlib.sha256\n    ).hexdigest()\n    return hmac.compare_digest(expected, signature)\n```\n\n---\n\n## SDKs\n\n### Official SDKs\n\n- **Python**: `pip install prooflink`\n- **JavaScript**: `npm install @prooflink/sdk`\n- **Ruby**: `gem install prooflink`\n- **PHP**: `composer require prooflink/sdk`\n- **Go**: `go get github.com/prooflink/go-sdk`\n\n### Community SDKs\n\n- **Java**: Available on Maven Central\n- **.NET**: Available on NuGet\n- **Rust**: Available on crates.io\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\n**Email**: api@prooflink.ai\n**Documentation**: https://docs.prooflink.ai\n**Status Page**: https://status.prooflink.ai\n**GitHub**: https://github.com/prooflink\n\n---\n\n*Last Updated: January 2024*\n*API Version: v1*\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Frontend Setup\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to frontend (new terminal)\ncd frontend\n\n# Install dependencies\nnpm install\n\n# Create .env.local file\ncp .env.example .env.local\n\n# Edit .env.local\nnano .env.local\n```\n\n**Required Environment Variables:**\n```env\nNEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://localhost:8000/api/v1\nNEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_test_...\n```\n\n**Start Frontend:**\n```bash\nnpm run dev\n```\n\n**Access:**\n- Frontend: http://localhost:3000\n\n---\n\n## Production Deployment\n\n### Option 1: Railway (Recommended)\n\n#### Backend Deployment\n\n1. **Install Railway CLI:**\n```bash\nnpm install -g @railway/cli\n```\n\n2. **Login to Railway:**\n```bash\nrailway login\n```\n\n3. **Create New Project:**\n```bash\nrailway init\n```\n\n4. **Add PostgreSQL:**\n```bash\nrailway add postgresql\n```\n\n5. **Set Environment Variables:**\n```bash\nrailway variables set SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key\nrailway variables set STRIPE_SECRET_KEY=sk_live_...\nrailway variables set STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_live_...\n# ... add all other variables\n```\n\n6. **Deploy Backend:**\n```bash\ncd backend\nrailway up\n```\n\n7. **Get Backend URL:**\n```bash\nrailway domain\n# Example: https://prooflink-backend.railway.app\n```\n\n#### Frontend Deployment (Vercel)\n\n1. **Install Vercel CLI:**\n```bash\nnpm install -g vercel\n```\n\n2. **Login to Vercel:**\n```bash\nvercel login\n```\n\n3. **Deploy Frontend:**\n```bash\ncd frontend\nvercel --prod\n```\n\n4. **Set Environment Variables in Vercel Dashboard:**\n- Go to https://vercel.com/dashboard\n- Select your project\n- Go to Settings ‚Üí Environment Variables\n- Add:\n  - `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL`: Your Railway backend URL\n  - `NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`: Your Stripe key\n\n5. **Redeploy:**\n```bash\nvercel --prod\n```\n\n### Option 2: Docker Deployment\n\n#### 1. Build Docker Images\n\n**Backend Dockerfile:**\n```dockerfile\nFROM python:3.11-slim\n\nWORKDIR /app\n\nCOPY requirements.txt .\nRUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt\n\nCOPY . .\n\nCMD ["uvicorn", "app.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"]\n```\n\n**Frontend Dockerfile:**\n```dockerfile\nFROM node:18-alpine\n\nWORKDIR /app\n\nCOPY package*.json ./\nRUN npm ci\n\nCOPY . .\nRUN npm run build\n\nCMD ["npm", "start"]\n```\n\n#### 2. Docker Compose\n\n```yaml\nversion: \'3.8\'\n\nservices:\n  postgres:\n    image: postgres:15\n    environment:\n      POSTGRES_DB: prooflink\n      POSTGRES_USER: prooflink\n      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: your-password\n    volumes:\n      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data\n    ports:\n      - "5432:5432"\n\n  redis:\n    image: redis:7-alpine\n    ports:\n      - "6379:6379"\n\n  backend:\n    build: ./backend\n    environment:\n      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://prooflink:your-password@postgres:5432/prooflink\n      SECRET_KEY: your-secret-key\n      STRIPE_SECRET_KEY: sk_live_...\n    ports:\n      - "8000:8000"\n    depends_on:\n      - postgres\n      - redis\n\n  frontend:\n    build: ./frontend\n    environment:\n      NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL: http://backend:8000/api/v1\n      NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY: pk_live_...\n    ports:\n      - "3000:3000"\n    depends_on:\n      - backend\n\nvolumes:\n  postgres_data:\n```\n\n**Deploy:**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n### Option 3: AWS Deployment\n\n#### Backend (AWS Elastic Beanstalk)\n\n1. **Install EB CLI:**\n```bash\npip install awsebcli\n```\n\n2. **Initialize EB:**\n```bash\ncd backend\neb init -p python-3.11 prooflink-backend\n```\n\n3. **Create Environment:**\n```bash\neb create prooflink-backend-prod\n```\n\n4. **Set Environment Variables:**\n```bash\neb setenv SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key \\\n  STRIPE_SECRET_KEY=sk_live_... \\\n  DATABASE_URL=postgresql://...\n```\n\n5. **Deploy:**\n```bash\neb deploy\n```\n\n#### Frontend (AWS Amplify)\n\n1. **Install Amplify CLI:**\n```bash\nnpm install -g @aws-amplify/cli\n```\n\n2. **Initialize Amplify:**\n```bash\ncd frontend\namplify init\n```\n\n3. **Add Hosting:**\n```bash\namplify add hosting\n```\n\n4. **Deploy:**\n```bash\namplify Backup Strategy\n\n**Daily Backups:**\n- Database: Automated daily backups\n- Files: S3 versioning enabled\n- Retention: 30 days\n\n**Disaster Recovery:**\n- RTO (Recovery Time Objective): 1 hour\n- RPO (Recovery Point Objective): 24 hours\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**1. Database Connection Error**\n```\nError: could not connect to server\n```\n**Solution:**\n- Check DATABASE_URL is correct\n- Verify database is running\n- Check firewall rules\n\n**2. CORS Error**\n```\nAccess to fetch blocked by CORS policy\n```\n**Solution:**\n- Add frontend URL to CORS origins\n- Check FRONTEND_URL environment variable\n\n**3. Stripe Webhook Error**\n```\nWebhook signature verification failed\n```\n**Solution:**\n- Verify STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET\n- Check webhook endpoint URL\n- Test with Stripe CLI\n\n**4. File Upload Error**\n```\nFile too large\n```\n**Solution:**\n- Check MAX_FILE_SIZE setting\n- Increase Nginx client_max_body_size\n- Update frontend file size limit\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\n**Documentation:** https://docs.prooflink.ai\n**Email:** support@prooflink.ai\n**Status Page:** https://status.prooflink.ai\n\n---\n\n*Last Updated: January 2024*\n*Version: 1.0.0*\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

\'pending\' as const,\n      progress: 0,\n    }));\n    setFiles((prev) => [...prev, ...newFiles]);\n  }, []);\n\n  const { getRootProps, getInputProps, isDragActive } = useDropzone({\n    onDrop,\n    multiple: true,\n  });\n\n  const createBatchProofs = useMutation({\n    mutationFn: async (filesToUpload: FileWithStatus[]) => {\n      setIsProcessing(true);\n      const results = [];\n\n =>\n            f.file === fileWithStatus.file\n              ? { ...f, status: \'uploading\' as const, progress: 0 }\n              : f\n          )\n        );\n\n        try {\n          const            )\n            );\n          }, 200);\n\n          const response = await api.post(\'/proofs\', formData, {\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'multipart/form-data\' },\n (\n        <Sun className="w-5 h-5 text-yellow-500" />\n      ) : (\n        <Moon className="w-5 h-5 text-gray-700" />\n      )}\n    </button>\n  );\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}
